sh-4.1$ #!/bin/bash
sh-4.1$ source  /afs/cern.ch/cms/cmsset_default.sh
sh-4.1$ export SCRAM_ARCH=slc6_amd64_gcc481
sh-4.1$ if [ -r CMSSW_7_1_16_patch1/src ] ; then 
>  echo release CMSSW_7_1_16_patch1 already exists
> else
> scram p CMSSW CMSSW_7_1_16_patch1
> fi
ml HIG-RunIIWinter15wmLHE-00488_1_cfg.py || exit $? ; 
echo 100 events were ran 
grep "TotalEvents" HIG-RunIIWinter15wmLHE-00488_rt.xml 
grep "Timing-tstoragefile-write-totalMegabytes" HIG-RunIIWinter15wmLHE-00488_rt.xml 
grep "PeakValueRss" HIG-RunIIWinter15wmLHE-00488_rt.xml 
grep "AvgEventTime" HIG-RunIIWinter15wmLHE-00488_rt.xml 
grep "AvgEventCPU" HIG-RunIIWinter15wmLHE-00488_rt.xml 
grep "TotalJobCPU" HIG-RunIIWinter15wmLHE-00488_rt.xml 

sh-4.1$ cd CMSSW_7_1_16_patch1/src
sh-4.1$ eval `scram runtime -sh`
sh-4.1$ 
sh-4.1$ curl -s --insecure https://cms-pdmv.cern.ch/mcm/public/restapi/requests/get_fragment/HIG-RunIIWinter15wmLHE-00488 --retry 2 --create-dirs -o Configuration/GenProduction/python/HIG-RunIIWinter15wmLHE-00488-fragment.py 
sh-4.1$ [ -s Configuration/GenProduction/python/HIG-RunIIWinter15wmLHE-00488-fragment.py ] || exit $?;
sh-4.1$ 
sh-4.1$ scram b
